# abap2UI5 — sample coverage

One row per UI5 demo kit sample, same layout as the in-system overview
app (`z2ui5_cl_api_app_overview`) — only the "start the app" link is
dropped, since this is a static page. **Control** links to the OpenUI5
API, **JavaScript** to the sample source in the
[OpenUI5 repository](https://github.com/SAP/openui5), **UI5 App** to the
live OpenUI5 fullscreen sample, **ABAP** to the generated class
(`—` = not ported yet). See the [README](README.md#coverage) for the
per-module coverage summary.

| Module | Control | Sample | JavaScript | UI5 App | ABAP |
|--------|---------|--------|:----------:|:-------:|:----:|
